{"answers": ["Middle Eastern alchemy"], "model_answer": "The term \"spirits\" for alcohol comes from Middle Eastern alchemy. In the Middle Ages, alchemists were concerned with medical elixirs rather than transmuting lead into gold. The vapor given off and collected during an alchemical process (such as distillation of alcohol) was called a spirit of the original material. This term \"spirit\" was later used to refer to the distilled essence of wine, which is now known as ethanol."}
